src/app/dashboard/page.tsx
'use client';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { Plus, Folder, Trash2, Code2, X, FileText } from 'lucide-react';
// Import the new UserMenu
import { UserMenu } from '@/components/ui/UserMenu';
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { apiClient } from '@/lib/api-client';


export default function DashboardPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [newProjectName, setNewProjectName] = useState('');
  const [description, setDescription] = useState(''); 
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const [projects, setProjects] = useState([
    { id: '1', name: 'Voice Agent V1', description: 'A voice assistant backend', updated: 'Just now' }
  ]);

  const handleCreateProject = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError('');

    if (!newProjectName.trim()) return setError('Project name is required');
    if (projects.some(p => p.name.toLowerCase() === newProjectName.toLowerCase())) return setError('Name exists');

    const newProject = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      name: newProjectName,
      description: description,
      updated: 'Just now'
    };

    setProjects([...projects, newProject]);
    setIsModalOpen(false);
    setNewProjectName('');
    setDescription('');
  };

  const handleDelete = (e: React.MouseEvent, id: string) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    if(confirm("Delete this project?")) {
      setProjects(projects.filter(p => p.id !== id));
    }
  };
  useEffect(() => {
    apiClient.getHealth().then((data) => {
      console.log("🔌 Backend Status:", data);
      if (data.status === 'online') {
        alert("System Connected: Frontend <-> Backend is LIVE!");
      }
    });
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 relative">
      {/* Header */}
      <header className="bg-white border-b border-gray-200 px-8 py-4 flex justify-between items-center sticky top-0 z-10">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
           <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-blue-600 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white shadow-md">
             <Code2 className="w-6 h-6" />
           </div>
           <span className="font-bold text-xl text-gray-800 tracking-tight">VoiceCode</span>
        </div>
        
        {/* ✅ Replaced "Sign Out" button with UserMenu */}
        <UserMenu />
      </header>

      <main className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-8 py-12">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-end mb-8">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900">Your Projects</h1>
            <p className="text-gray-500 mt-2">Manage your workspaces</p>
          </div>
          <button 
            onClick={() => setIsModalOpen(true)}
            className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-gray-900 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-xl hover:bg-gray-800 shadow-lg active:scale-95 transition-all font-medium"
          >
            <Plus className="w-5 h-5" /> New Project
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {projects.map((project) => (
            <div 
              key={project.id} 
              onClick={() => router.push(`/editor/${project.id}`)}
              className="group bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-gray-100 hover:border-blue-500 hover:shadow-xl transition-all cursor-pointer relative flex flex-col h-[160px]"
            >
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-blue-50 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-blue-600">
                  <Folder className="w-6 h-6 fill-current" />
                </div>
                <button onClick={(e) => handleDelete(e, project.id)} className="p-2 text-gray-300 hover:text-red-500 hover:bg-red-50 rounded-lg transition-colors">
                  <Trash2 className="w-4 h-4" />
                </button>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex-1">
                <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-gray-900 mb-1 truncate">{project.name}</h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 line-clamp-2 h-8 leading-relaxed">
                    {project.description || "No description provided."}
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </main>

      {/* CREATE MODAL */}
      {isModalOpen && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4">
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-md p-6 animate-in fade-in zoom-in duration-200">
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-900">Create Workspace</h2>
              <button onClick={() => setIsModalOpen(false)} className="p-2 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-full text-gray-500"><X className="w-5 h-5" /></button>
            </div>
            
            <form onSubmit={handleCreateProject} className="space-y-5">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1.5">Project Name</label>
                <input autoFocus type="text" value={newProjectName} onChange={(e) => setNewProjectName(e.target.value)} placeholder="e.g., Trading Bot" className="w-full px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 outline-none" />
              </div>
              <div>
                 <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1.5">Description</label>
                 <div className="relative">
                    <FileText className="absolute left-4 top-3.5 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
                    <textarea value={description} onChange={(e) => setDescription(e.target.value)} placeholder="Describe your app..." className="w-full pl-12 pr-4 py-3 rounded-xl border border-gray-200 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 outline-none min-h-[120px] resize-none" />
                 </div>
              </div>
              {error && <p className="text-red-500 text-sm bg-red-50 p-2 rounded-lg">{error}</p>}
              <div className="flex gap-3 pt-2">
                <button type="button" onClick={() => setIsModalOpen(false)} className="flex-1 px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 text-gray-700 rounded-xl font-medium hover:bg-gray-100">Cancel</button>
                <button type="submit" className="flex-1 px-4 py-3 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-xl font-medium hover:bg-blue-700 shadow-md">Create Project</button>
              </div>
            </form>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

src/app/editor/[projectId]/page.tsx
"use client";

import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { Panel, PanelGroup, PanelResizeHandle } from "react-resizable-panels";
import CodeEditor from "@/components/ui/CodeEditor";
import AgentChatPanel from "@/features/agent/components/AgentChatPanel";
import FileTree from "@/components/layouts/FileTree";
import { useWakeWord } from "@/features/agent/hooks/useWakeWord";
import { Mic, Zap } from "lucide-react";

export default function EditorPage() {
  // STATE
  const [leftOpen, setLeftOpen] = useState(true);
  const [rightOpen, setRightOpen] = useState(true);
  const [files, setFiles] = useState([]); // This would be populated by fetching /files/tree
  
  // VOICE
  const { isWakeWordDetected, startWakeWord, setIsWakeWordDetected } = useWakeWord();

  useEffect(() => {
    startWakeWord(); // Start Picovoice on Load
    // fetchFiles(); // You need to implement this fetch
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="h-screen w-full bg-[#1e1e1e] text-gray-300 flex flex-col overflow-hidden">
      
      {/* 1. TOP BAR */}
      <div className="h-10 bg-[#18181b] flex items-center justify-between px-4 border-b border-[#2a2d2e] select-none">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <Zap size={16} className="text-yellow-500" />
            <span className="text-sm font-bold">Cursor Clone</span>
        </div>
        
        {/* Wake Word Status */}
        <div className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs font-mono flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${isWakeWordDetected ? "bg-red-500/20 text-red-400" : "bg-gray-800"}`}>
            <Mic size={12} className={isWakeWordDetected ? "animate-pulse" : ""} />
            {isWakeWordDetected ? "LISTENING..." : "Waiting for 'Jarvis'"}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 2. MAIN RESIZABLE AREA */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex overflow-hidden">
        <PanelGroup direction="horizontal">
            
            {/* LEFT SIDEBAR (FILE EXPLORER) */}
            {leftOpen && (
                <>
                <Panel defaultSize={20} minSize={10} collapsible={true} onCollapse={() => setLeftOpen(false)}>
                    <div className="h-full flex flex-col bg-[#18181b]">
                        <div className="p-2 text-xs font-bold tracking-wider text-gray-500 flex justify-between">
                            EXPLORER
                            <div className="flex gap-2">
                                <FilePlus size={14} className="cursor-pointer hover:text-white"/>
                                <FolderPlus size={14} className="cursor-pointer hover:text-white"/>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto">
                            <FileTree data={files} onFileSelect={(f) => console.log("Open", f)} />
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </Panel>
                <PanelResizeHandle className="w-1 bg-[#2a2d2e] hover:bg-blue-600 transition" />
                </>
            )}

            {/* CENTER (EDITOR) */}
            <Panel minSize={30}>
                <CodeEditor code="# Click a file to edit..." onChange={() => {}} />
            </Panel>

            {/* RIGHT SIDEBAR (AI CHAT) */}
            {rightOpen && (
                <>
                <PanelResizeHandle className="w-1 bg-[#2a2d2e] hover:bg-blue-600 transition" />
                <Panel defaultSize={25} minSize={15} collapsible={true} onCollapse={() => setRightOpen(false)}>
                    <AgentChatPanel 
                        messages={[]} 
                        onSendMessage={() => {}} 
                        isProcessing={false} 
                    />
                </Panel>
                </>
            )}

        </PanelGroup>
      </div>

      {/* 3. FOOTER (Toggle Buttons) */}
      <div className="h-6 bg-[#007acc] text-white flex items-center px-2 text-xs justify-between">
         <div className="flex gap-4">
             <button onClick={() => setLeftOpen(!leftOpen)}>Toggle Sidebar</button>
         </div>
         <div className="flex gap-4">
             <button onClick={() => setRightOpen(!rightOpen)}>Toggle AI Chat</button>
         </div>
      </div>

    </div>
  );
}

src/app/globals.css 
@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

:root {
  --background: 255 255 255;
  --foreground: 17 24 39;
}

/* When the "dark" class is present, swap the variables */
.dark {
  --background: 17 24 39; /* Dark Gray */
  --foreground: 255 255 255;
}

body {
  /* Use the variables */
  background-color: rgb(var(--background));
  color: rgb(var(--foreground));
  transition: background-color 0.3s ease, color 0.3s ease;
}

/* Optional: Make cards dark in dark mode */
.dark .bg-white {
    background-color: #1f2937; /* Gray-800 */
    color: white;
    border-color: #374151; /* Gray-700 */
}

.dark .text-gray-900 {
    color: white;
}

src/components/layouts/FileTree.tsx 
import { useState } from "react";
import { 
  ChevronRight, ChevronDown, FileCode, Folder, FolderOpen, 
  MoreVertical, Trash, Edit, FilePlus, FolderPlus 
} from "lucide-react";
import { ContextMenu, ContextMenuTrigger, ContextMenuContent, ContextMenuItem } from "@/components/ui/context-menu"; // Assuming you have shadcn or similar, OR use raw divs

// SIMPLE RECURSIVE FILE TREE ITEM
const FileTreeItem = ({ item, level, onSelect, onAction }: any) => {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const isFolder = item.type === "directory";
  
  const handleToggle = (e: any) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    if (isFolder) setIsOpen(!isOpen);
    else onSelect(item.path);
  };

  return (
    <div className="text-gray-300 select-none">
        <div 
          className={`flex items-center gap-1 py-1 px-2 hover:bg-[#2a2d2e] cursor-pointer ${level > 0 ? "ml-4" : ""}`}
          onClick={handleToggle}
          onContextMenu={(e) => {
              e.preventDefault();
              // In a real app, you trigger a custom context menu state here
              // For MVP: We will just show a tiny action button on hover
          }}
        >
            <span className="opacity-70">
                {isFolder ? (isOpen ? <ChevronDown size={14} /> : <ChevronRight size={14} />) : <div className="w-3.5" />}
            </span>
            
            {isFolder ? (
               isOpen ? <FolderOpen size={16} className="text-blue-400" /> : <Folder size={16} className="text-blue-400" />
            ) : (
               <FileCode size={16} className="text-yellow-400" />
            )}
            
            <span className="text-sm truncate ml-1">{item.name}</span>
            
            {/* QUICK ACTIONS (Replaces Right Click for MVP Simplicity) */}
            <div className="ml-auto flex gap-1 opacity-0 hover:opacity-100 group-hover:opacity-100">
                <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onAction("delete", item.path); }}><Trash size={12} className="text-red-400" /></button>
            </div>
        </div>

        {isFolder && isOpen && item.children && (
            <div>
                {item.children.map((child: any) => (
                    <FileTreeItem key={child.path} item={child} level={level + 1} onSelect={onSelect} onAction={onAction} />
                ))}
            </div>
        )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default function FileTree({ data, onFileSelect, refreshTree }: any) {
  const handleAction = async (action: string, path: string) => {
      // Call your new API endpoints here
      if (action === "delete") {
          if(!confirm("Delete " + path + "?")) return;
          await fetch("http://localhost:8000/files/delete?path=" + path, { method: "DELETE" });
          refreshTree();
      }
  };

  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      {data.map((item: any) => (
        <FileTreeItem key={item.path} item={item} level={0} onSelect={onFileSelect} onAction={handleAction} />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

src/components/layouts/Sidebar.tsx
import { FolderOpen, FileCode, Settings, ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from "lucide-react";
import { useState } from "react";

export default function Sidebar({ isOpen, toggle }: { isOpen: boolean, toggle: () => void }) {
  return (
    <div className={`bg-[#18181b] border-r border-[#27272a] flex flex-col transition-all duration-300 ${isOpen ? "w-64" : "w-12"}`}>
      {/* TOGGLE BUTTON */}
      <div className="h-10 flex items-center justify-end px-2 border-b border-[#27272a]">
        <button onClick={toggle} className="text-gray-500 hover:text-white">
            {isOpen ? <ChevronLeft size={16} /> : <ChevronRight size={16} />}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* CONTENT */}
      {isOpen ? (
        <div className="p-4">
            <div className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 mb-4">EXPLORER</div>
            <div className="space-y-1">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-blue-400 bg-[#27272a] p-2 rounded cursor-pointer">
                    <FileCode size={14} /> main.py
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-400 hover:text-white p-2 rounded cursor-pointer">
                    <FileCode size={14} /> utils.py
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center pt-4 gap-4">
            <FolderOpen size={20} className="text-gray-500" />
            <Settings size={20} className="text-gray-500" />
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

src/components/ui/button.tsx
import * as React from 'react';
import { cva, type VariantProps } from 'class-variance-authority';
import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

// The "Recipe" for a button
const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-1 focus-visible:ring-blue-500 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-blue-600 text-white hover:bg-blue-700 shadow-sm",
        destructive: "bg-red-500 text-white hover:bg-red-600 shadow-sm",
        outline: "border border-gray-200 bg-white hover:bg-gray-100 hover:text-gray-900",
        ghost: "hover:bg-gray-100 hover:text-gray-900",
        link: "text-blue-600 underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-10 px-4 py-2",
        sm: "h-8 rounded-md px-3 text-xs",
        lg: "h-12 rounded-md px-8 text-base",
        icon: "h-10 w-10",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
);

// Interface extension ensures we get all standard HTML button props (onClick, type, etc.)
export interface ButtonProps
  extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  isLoading?: boolean;
}

export const Button = React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  ({ className, variant, size, isLoading, children, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <button
        className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
        ref={ref}
        disabled={isLoading || props.disabled}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" />}
        {children}
      </button>
    );
  }
);
Button.displayName = "Button";

'use client';
import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { LogOut, Settings, Moon, Sun, Monitor, User, CreditCard } from 'lucide-react';
import { useTheme } from '@/context/ThemeContext';
import { useUser } from '@/context/UserContext';

export function UserMenu() {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const router = useRouter();
  
  // 1. Get Theme and User Data
  const { theme, setTheme } = useTheme();
  const { user } = useUser(); 

  // 2. Define the missing 'menuRef'
  const menuRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // 3. Close menu when clicking outside
  useEffect(() => {
    function handleClickOutside(event: MouseEvent) {
      if (menuRef.current && !menuRef.current.contains(event.target as Node)) {
        setIsOpen(false);
      }
    }
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, [menuRef]);

  return (
    <div className="relative" ref={menuRef}>
      {/* Avatar Button */}
      <button 
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(!isOpen)}
        className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-tr from-blue-600 to-purple-600 flex items-center justify-center text-white font-medium shadow-sm hover:ring-2 hover:ring-offset-2 hover:ring-blue-500 transition-all"
      >
        {/* Shows AJ if name is Adeel Jutt */}
        {user.initials}
      </button>

      {/* Dropdown Menu */}
      {isOpen && (
        <div className="absolute right-0 top-12 w-72 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl border border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700 p-4 z-50 animate-in fade-in zoom-in-95 duration-100 origin-top-right">
          
          {/* Header Section */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4 pb-4 border-b border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700">
             <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-blue-50 dark:bg-blue-900/30 flex items-center justify-center text-blue-600 dark:text-blue-400 font-bold text-lg">
               {user.initials}
             </div>
             <div>
               <h4 className="font-semibold text-gray-900 dark:text-white">{user.name}</h4>
               <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">{user.email}</p>
             </div>
          </div>

          {/* Theme Toggle */}
          <div className="mb-4">
            <label className="text-xs font-semibold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider mb-2 block px-1">Theme</label>
            <div className="flex bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 p-1 rounded-xl">
               <button onClick={() => setTheme('light')} className={`flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-lg transition-all ${theme === 'light' ? 'bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm' : 'text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-700'}`}>
                 <Sun className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Light
               </button>
               <button onClick={() => setTheme('dark')} className={`flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-lg transition-all ${theme === 'dark' ? 'bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm' : 'text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-700'}`}>
                 <Moon className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Dark
               </button>
               <button onClick={() => setTheme('system')} className={`flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium rounded-lg transition-all ${theme === 'system' ? 'bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm' : 'text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-700'}`}>
                 <Monitor className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Auto
               </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Menu Items */}
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700/50 rounded-lg transition-colors">
              <User className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" /> Manage Account
            </button>
            <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700/50 rounded-lg transition-colors">
              <CreditCard className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" /> Subscription
            </button>
            <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-50 dark:hover:bg-gray-700/50 rounded-lg transition-colors">
              <Settings className="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400" /> Settings
            </button>
          </div>

          <div className="border-t border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-700 mt-4 pt-2">
            <button 
              onClick={() => router.push('/signin')}
              className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-red-600 hover:bg-red-50 dark:hover:bg-red-900/20 rounded-lg transition-colors"
            >
              <LogOut className="w-4 h-4" /> Sign Out
            </button>
          </div>

        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

src/context/EditorContext.tsx 
'use client';
import { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react';

// Types
export interface FileNode {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'folder';
  children?: FileNode[];
  content?: string;
}

interface EditorContextType {
  files: FileNode[];
  activeFileId: string | null;
  code: string;
  setFiles: (files: FileNode[]) => void;
  setActiveFileId: (id: string | null) => void;
  setCode: (code: string) => void;
  createFile: (name: string, content?: string) => void;
  renameNode: (id: string, newName: string) => void;
}

const EditorContext = createContext<EditorContextType | undefined>(undefined);

const STORAGE_KEY = 'voicecode_workspace_v1';

export function EditorProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  // Initialize state
  const [files, setFiles] = useState<FileNode[]>([]);
  const [activeFileId, setActiveFileId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
  const [isLoaded, setIsLoaded] = useState(false);

  // 1. HYDRATION: Load from LocalStorage on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    if (saved) {
      try {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);
        setFiles(parsed);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error("Failed to load workspace:", e);
      }
    }
    setIsLoaded(true);
  }, []);

  // 2. PERSISTENCE: Auto-save whenever files change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isLoaded) {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(files));
    }
  }, [files, isLoaded]);

  // Helper: Recursive Check
  const exists = (nodes: FileNode[], name: string): boolean => {
    return nodes.some(n => n.name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase());
  };

  const createFile = (name: string, content: string = '') => {
    if (exists(files, name)) {
      alert(`Error: "${name}" already exists.`);
      return; 
    }
    const newFile: FileNode = { id: Date.now().toString(), name, type: 'file', content };
    setFiles((prev) => [...prev, newFile]);
    setActiveFileId(newFile.id);
    setCode(content);
  };

  const renameNode = (id: string, newName: string) => {
    if (!newName.trim()) return;
    if (exists(files, newName)) {
        alert(`Error: "${newName}" already exists.`);
        return;
    }
    const updateRecursive = (nodes: FileNode[]): FileNode[] => {
      return nodes.map(node => {
        if (node.id === id) return { ...node, name: newName };
        if (node.children) return { ...node, children: updateRecursive(node.children) };
        return node;
      });
    };
    setFiles(prev => updateRecursive(prev));
  };

  // 3. Prevent rendering children until hydration is complete to avoid "Hydration Mismatch"
  if (!isLoaded) {
    return null; // Or a loading spinner
  }

  return (
    <EditorContext.Provider value={{ 
      files, activeFileId, code, 
      setFiles, setActiveFileId, setCode, 
      createFile, renameNode 
    }}>
      {children}
    </EditorContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useEditor = () => {
  const context = useContext(EditorContext);
  if (!context) throw new Error('useEditor must be used within EditorProvider');
  return context;
};  

src/context/ThemeContext.tsx 
'use client';
import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';

type Theme = 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';

interface ThemeContextType {
  theme: Theme;
  setTheme: (theme: Theme) => void;
}

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export function ThemeProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>('system');

  useEffect(() => {
    const root = window.document.documentElement;
    root.classList.remove('light', 'dark');

    if (theme === 'system') {
      const systemTheme = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches ? 'dark' : 'light';
      root.classList.add(systemTheme);
      return;
    }

    root.classList.add(theme);
  }, [theme]);

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useTheme = () => {
  const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (context === undefined) throw new Error('useTheme must be used within a ThemeProvider');
  return context;
};

src/context/UserContext.tsx
'use client';
import { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';

// Define what a User looks like
interface UserProfile {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  initials: string;
}

interface UserContextType {
  user: UserProfile;
  updateUser: (name: string) => void;
}

const UserContext = createContext<UserContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export function UserProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  // Default State (Mock Data)
  const [user, setUser] = useState<UserProfile>({
    name: 'Adeel Jutt', // ✅ Default Name
    email: 'adeel@example.com',
    initials: 'AJ'
  });

  // Helper to update name and auto-calculate initials
  const updateUser = (newName: string) => {
    const initials = newName
      .split(' ')
      .map((n) => n[0])
      .join('')
      .toUpperCase()
      .substring(0, 2);
      
    setUser({ ...user, name: newName, initials });
  };

  return (
    <UserContext.Provider value={{ user, updateUser }}>
      {children}
    </UserContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useUser = () => {
  const context = useContext(UserContext);
  if (context === undefined) throw new Error('useUser must be used within UserProvider');
  return context;
};

src/features/agent/components/AgentChatPanel.
"use client";
import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { Send, Bot, User, Mic } from "lucide-react";

interface Message {
  role: "user" | "assistant";
  text: string;
}

interface AgentChatPanelProps {
  messages: Message[];
  onSendMessage: (msg: string) => void;
  isProcessing: boolean;
}

export default function AgentChatPanel({ messages, onSendMessage, isProcessing }: AgentChatPanelProps) {
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // Auto-scroll to bottom
  useEffect(() => {
    if (scrollRef.current) {
      scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
    }
  }, [messages]);

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (!input.trim()) return;
    onSendMessage(input);
    setInput("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full bg-[#18181b] border-l border-[#27272a]">
      {/* HEADER */}
      <div className="p-3 border-b border-[#27272a] flex justify-between items-center bg-[#18181b]">
        <h2 className="text-xs font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">AI Copilot</h2>
        <span className="text-[10px] bg-blue-900 text-blue-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full">Beta</span>
      </div>

      {/* CHAT HISTORY */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4" ref={scrollRef}>
        {messages.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center text-gray-600 mt-10 text-sm">
            <p>Ready to code.</p>
            <p>Say <span className="text-blue-400">"Jarvis"</span> or type below.</p>
          </div>
        )}
        
        {messages.map((msg, i) => (
          <div key={i} className={`flex gap-3 ${msg.role === "user" ? "flex-row-reverse" : ""}`}>
            <div className={`w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${msg.role === "user" ? "bg-blue-600" : "bg-purple-600"}`}>
              {msg.role === "user" ? <User size={14} /> : <Bot size={14} />}
            </div>
            <div className={`p-3 rounded-lg text-sm max-w-[85%] leading-relaxed ${msg.role === "user" ? "bg-blue-900/30 text-blue-100" : "bg-[#27272a] text-gray-200"}`}>
              {msg.text}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
        
        {isProcessing && (
          <div className="flex gap-3">
             <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-purple-600 flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse"><Bot size={14} /></div>
             <div className="text-gray-500 text-sm flex items-center">Thinking...</div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* INPUT AREA */}
      <div className="p-4 border-t border-[#27272a] bg-[#18181b]">
        <div className="relative">
          <textarea
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey && (e.preventDefault(), handleSend())}
            placeholder="Ask AI to edit code or explain..."
            className="w-full bg-[#27272a] text-gray-200 text-sm rounded-md p-3 pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500 resize-none h-20"
          />
          <button 
            onClick={handleSend}
            disabled={isProcessing || !input.trim()}
            className="absolute bottom-3 right-3 text-gray-400 hover:text-white disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            <Send size={16} />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

src/features/agent/components/AgentPanel.
'use client';
import { useRef, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { Mic, Send, Sparkles, StopCircle, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';
import { useVoiceAgent } from '../hooks/useVoiceAgent';
import { useEditor } from '@/context/EditorContext';

export function AgentPanel() {
  const { state, messages, transcript, startListening, stopListening } = useVoiceAgent();
  const bottomRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [inputText, setInputText] = useState('');
  const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);
  
  const { createFile } = useEditor();

  useEffect(() => {
    bottomRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [messages, transcript]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (textareaRef.current) {
      textareaRef.current.style.height = 'auto';
      textareaRef.current.style.height = textareaRef.current.scrollHeight + 'px';
    }
  }, [inputText]);

  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
      e.preventDefault();
      
      if (state === 'LISTENING') {
        stopListening();
      } 
      else if (inputText.trim()) {
        processCommand(inputText);
        setInputText('');
      }
    }
  };

  const processCommand = (text: string) => {
    const lower = text.toLowerCase();

    // 1. Check if user wants to create a file
    if (lower.includes('create')) {
      let fileName = 'untitled.txt';
      let content = ''; // ✅ Default: EMPTY

      // 2. Detect Language for File Extension
      if (lower.includes('python')) {
        fileName = 'main.py';
      } 
      else if (lower.includes('javascript') || lower.includes('js')) {
        fileName = 'index.js';
      }
      else if (lower.includes('java')) {
        fileName = 'Main.java';
      }
      else if (lower.includes('c++') || lower.includes('cpp')) {
        fileName = 'main.cpp';
      }
      else if (lower.includes('react')) {
        fileName = 'Component.tsx';
      }
      else if (lower.includes('html')) {
        fileName = 'index.html';
      }
      else if (lower.includes('css')) {
        fileName = 'style.css';
      }

      // 3. Only add content if EXPLICITLY requested
      const wantsContent = 
        lower.includes('with code') || 
        lower.includes('template') || 
        lower.includes('hello world') || 
        lower.includes('boilerplate') ||
        lower.includes('example');

      if (wantsContent) {
        if (fileName.endsWith('.py')) content = 'print("Hello World")';
        if (fileName.endsWith('.js')) content = 'console.log("Hello World");';
        if (fileName.endsWith('.java')) content = 'public class Main {\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        System.out.println("Hello");\n    }\n}';
        if (fileName.endsWith('.cpp')) content = '#include <iostream>\nint main() { return 0; }';
        if (fileName.endsWith('.tsx')) content = 'export const Component = () => <div>Hello</div>;';
        if (fileName.endsWith('.html')) content = '<html><body><h1>Hello</h1></body></html>';
      }

      // 4. Create the file
      createFile(fileName, content);
      
      const responseMsg = wantsContent 
        ? `Agent: "Created ${fileName} with starter code."`
        : `Agent: "Created empty file: ${fileName}"`;
        
      alert(responseMsg);

    } else {
      // Normal Chat (Mock)
      alert(`Agent: "I received: ${text}"`);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 relative transition-colors">
      
      {/* 1. Chat History */}
      <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-6">
        {messages.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center mt-10 space-y-2 opacity-50 dark:opacity-40">
            <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-gradient-to-tr from-blue-500 to-purple-500 rounded-xl mx-auto flex items-center justify-center text-white mb-4">
              <Sparkles className="w-6 h-6" />
            </div>
            <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-300">"Help me refactor main.py"</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {messages.map((msg) => (
          <div key={msg.id} className={cn("flex gap-3", msg.role === 'user' ? "flex-row-reverse" : "")}>
            <div className={cn(
              "w-8 h-8 rounded-full flex-shrink-0 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold",
              msg.role === 'agent' ? "bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-600 to-purple-600 text-white" : "bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300"
            )}>
              {msg.role === 'agent' ? 'AI' : 'YOU'}
            </div>
            <div className={cn(
              "p-3 rounded-2xl text-sm max-w-[85%] leading-relaxed",
              msg.role === 'agent' ? "bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-800 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 rounded-tl-none" : "bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-tr-none"
            )}>
              {msg.content}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {state !== 'IDLE' && (
          <div className="flex gap-3 animate-pulse">
            <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700" />
            <div className="p-3 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-2xl text-sm text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 italic">
              {state === 'LISTENING' ? (transcript || "Listening...") : "Thinking..."}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
        <div ref={bottomRef} />
      </div>

      {/* 2. Input Bar (Auto-Growing) */}
      <div className="p-4 bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 border-t border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800">
        <div className={cn(
          "relative flex items-end gap-2 p-2 rounded-3xl border transition-all duration-300",
          state === 'LISTENING' 
            ? "border-red-300 ring-4 ring-red-50 bg-red-50/10" 
            : "border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-800 focus-within:ring-2 focus-within:ring-blue-100 dark:focus-within:ring-blue-900/30 focus-within:bg-white dark:focus-within:bg-gray-800"
        )}>
          
          <textarea 
            ref={textareaRef}
            value={inputText}
            onChange={(e) => setInputText(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            placeholder={state === 'LISTENING' ? "Listening..." : "Ask anything..."}
            className="flex-1 max-h-48 min-h-[44px] py-3 px-3 bg-transparent border-none outline-none text-sm resize-none overflow-y-auto text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-100 placeholder:text-gray-400 dark:placeholder:text-gray-500"
            rows={1}
            disabled={state !== 'IDLE'}
          />

          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 pb-1 pr-1">
             {state === 'IDLE' ? (
               <button 
                 onClick={startListening}
                 className="p-3 rounded-full bg-gray-900 dark:bg-white text-white dark:text-gray-900 hover:opacity-90 transition-transform active:scale-95 shadow-md"
               >
                 <Mic className="w-5 h-5" />
               </button>
             ) : state === 'LISTENING' ? (
                <button 
                  onClick={stopListening}
                  className="p-3 rounded-full bg-red-500 text-white hover:bg-red-600 transition-all animate-pulse shadow-red-200 shadow-lg"
                >
                  <StopCircle className="w-5 h-5 fill-current" />
                </button>
             ) : (
                <button disabled className="p-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-400">
                  <Loader2 className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin" />
                </button>
             )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
 
 src/features/agent/hooks/useVoiceAgent.ts 
 import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import 'regenerator-runtime/runtime';
import SpeechRecognition, { useSpeechRecognition } from 'react-speech-recognition';

export const useVoiceAgent = () => {
  const [isWakeWordDetected, setIsWakeWordDetected] = useState(false);
  const [status, setStatus] = useState("Idle");
  const silenceTimer = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout | null>(null);
  
  const {
    transcript,
    resetTranscript,
    listening,
    browserSupportsSpeechRecognition
  } = useSpeechRecognition();

  // 1. IMMORTAL LISTENING LOOP
  // If the browser stops listening but we didn't ask it to, RESTART IT.
  useEffect(() => {
     if (!listening && status !== "Idle") {
         SpeechRecognition.startListening({ continuous: true, language: 'en-US' });
     }
  }, [listening, status]);

  const startListening = () => {
    setStatus("Listening for 'Jarvis'...");
    SpeechRecognition.startListening({ continuous: true, language: 'en-US' });
  };

  const stopListening = () => {
    setStatus("Idle");
    SpeechRecognition.stopListening();
  };

  // 2. WAKE WORD LOGIC
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!transcript) return;
    const lower = transcript.toLowerCase();

    // TRIGGER: "JARVIS"
    if (!isWakeWordDetected && lower.includes("jarvis")) {
        setIsWakeWordDetected(true);
        setStatus("Listening for command...");
        resetTranscript(); // Clear "Jarvis" from buffer
    }

    // COMMAND CAPTURE (After Wake Word)
    if (isWakeWordDetected && transcript.length > 5) {
        // Debounce: Wait 2.5s for silence before sending
        if (silenceTimer.current) clearTimeout(silenceTimer.current);
        
        silenceTimer.current = setTimeout(() => {
            console.log("🎤 COMMAND LOCKED:", transcript);
            // We don't execute here, we let the component read the transcript
        }, 2500);
    }
  }, [transcript, isWakeWordDetected]);

  return { 
    isListening: listening, 
    transcript, 
    startListening, 
    stopListening,
    status,
    isWakeWordDetected,
    setIsWakeWordDetected, // Allow component to reset after sending
    resetTranscript
  };
};

 src/features/agent/hooks/useWakeWord.ts
 import { usePorcupine } from "@picovoice/porcupine-react";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";

// You can use the standard "Jarvis" keyword provided by Picovoice or train your own.
const JARVIS_KEYWORD = { publicPath: "/keywords/jarvis_wasm.ppn", label: "jarvis" }; // You will need to download the .ppn file or use the built-in 'Jarvis' if available in their default list.
// FOR MVP: Use the built-in "Porcupine" or "Jarvis" keyword model provided in the SDK docs.

export const useWakeWord = () => {
  const [isWakeWordDetected, setIsWakeWordDetected] = useState(false);
  
  const {
    keywordDetection,
    isLoaded,
    isListening,
    error,
    start,
    stop,
  } = usePorcupine({
    accessKey: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_PICOVOICE_KEY || "", // READ FROM ENV
    keyword: { builtin: "Jarvis" }, // Use Built-in Jarvis
    onDetection: () => {
      console.log("🔥 JARVIS HEARD!");
      setIsWakeWordDetected(true);
    },
  });

  return {
    isWakeWordDetected,
    setIsWakeWordDetected,
    startWakeWord: start,
    stopWakeWord: stop,
    isLoaded,
    error
  };
};

 src/features/agent/services/agentService.ts
 import axios from 'axios';

// Ensure this matches your FastAPI port (usually 8000)
const API_URL = "http://localhost:8000";

export const agentService = {
  /**
   * Sends a natural language command to the AI to edit a specific file.
   */
  executeEdit: async (instruction: string, filename: string, currentContent: string) => {
    try {
      const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/agent/edit`, {
        instruction,
        filename,
        current_content: currentContent
      });
      
      return response.data; // Expecting { status: "success", new_content: "..." }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Agent Service Error:", error);
      throw error;
    }
  },

  /**
   * (Optional) Health check to see if backend is alive
   */
  checkHealth: async () => {
    return axios.get(`${API_URL}/`);
  }
};


src/features/editor/components/EditorLayout.tsx 
'use client';
import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { Panel, PanelGroup, PanelResizeHandle } from 'react-resizable-panels';
import { MonacoWrapper } from './MonacoWrapper';
import { FileTree } from './FileTree';
import { AgentPanel } from '../../agent/components/AgentPanel';
import { FilePlus, FolderPlus, Trash2, Sidebar, PanelRightClose, Edit2 } from 'lucide-react'; 
import { useEditor } from '@/context/EditorContext';
import { fileService } from '../services/fileService'; // <--- 1. MAKE SURE THIS IMPORT EXISTS

export function EditorLayout() {
  const { files, activeFileId, code, setFiles, setActiveFileId, setCode, createFile, renameNode } = useEditor();
  
  const [leftCollapsed, setLeftCollapsed] = useState(false);
  const [rightCollapsed, setRightCollapsed] = useState(false);
  const leftPanelRef = useRef<any>(null);
  const rightPanelRef = useRef<any>(null);

  const handleCreateFile = () => {
    const name = prompt("File Name:");
    if (name) createFile(name, ""); 
  };

  const handleCreateFolder = () => {
    const name = prompt("Folder Name:");
    if (files.some(f => f.name === name)) return alert("Folder exists!");
    if (name) setFiles([...files, { id: Date.now().toString(), name, type: 'folder', children: [] }]);
  };

  const handleDelete = () => {
    if(!activeFileId) return alert("Select a file to delete");
    setFiles(files.filter(f => f.id !== activeFileId));
    setActiveFileId(null);
    setCode("");
  };

  const handleRename = () => {
    if(!activeFileId) return alert("Select a file to rename");
    const currentFile = files.find(f => f.id === activeFileId);
    if (!currentFile) return;

    const newName = prompt("Rename to:", currentFile.name);
    if (newName && newName !== currentFile.name) {
        renameNode(activeFileId, newName);
    }
  };

  return (
     <div className="h-full w-full bg-white dark:bg-gray-900 flex flex-col transition-colors duration-300">
       {/* 1. TOP STATUS BAR */}
       <div className="h-10 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-900 border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 flex items-center justify-between px-4 shrink-0">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button onClick={() => { const p = leftPanelRef.current; leftCollapsed ? p?.expand() : p?.collapse(); }} className="p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-gray-200 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 text-blue-600 dark:text-blue-400">
                <Sidebar className="w-4 h-4" />
            </button>
            <span className="text-xs font-mono text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400">Workspace</span>
          </div>
          <button onClick={() => { const p = rightPanelRef.current; rightCollapsed ? p?.expand() : p?.collapse(); }} className="p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-gray-200 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 text-blue-600 dark:text-blue-400">
                <PanelRightClose className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>
       </div>

       {/* 2. MAIN LAYOUT */}
       <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
        <PanelGroup direction="horizontal">
            {/* LEFT */}
            <Panel ref={leftPanelRef} defaultSize={20} minSize={10} collapsible onCollapse={() => setLeftCollapsed(true)} onExpand={() => setLeftCollapsed(false)} className="bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-900 border-r border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 flex flex-col">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-1 p-2 border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 shrink-0">
                    <button title="New File" onClick={handleCreateFile} className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-200 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 rounded text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400"><FilePlus className="w-4 h-4"/></button>
                    <button title="New Folder" onClick={handleCreateFolder} className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-200 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 rounded text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400"><FolderPlus className="w-4 h-4"/></button>
                    <button title="Rename" onClick={handleRename} className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-200 dark:hover:bg-gray-800 rounded text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400"><Edit2 className="w-4 h-4"/></button>
                    <button title="Delete" onClick={handleDelete} className="p-1 hover:bg-red-100 dark:hover:bg-red-900/30 text-gray-400 hover:text-red-500 rounded"><Trash2 className="w-4 h-4"/></button>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1 overflow-auto p-2 cursor-default" onClick={() => { setActiveFileId(null); setCode(""); }}>
        <FileTree 
                data={files} 
                activeFileId={activeFileId} 
                onSelect={async (node) => {
                    // 1. Highlight the file
                    setActiveFileId(node.id);
                    
                // 2. Fetch the content (The Missing Link)
                if (node.type === 'file') {
                    try {
                        // Use the new endpoint we added to main.py
                        // NOTE: backend URL is usually port 8000
                        const res = await fetch(`http://localhost:8000/read_file?path=${node.name}`);
                        
                        if (!res.ok) throw new Error("File fetch failed");
                        
                        const data = await res.json();
                        setCode(data.content || ""); 
                        
                    } catch (err) {
                        console.error("Error loading file:", err);
                        setCode("// Error: Could not load file from backend.");
                    }
                }
            }} 
        />
                </div>
            </Panel>
            
            <PanelResizeHandle className="w-1 hover:bg-blue-500 transition-colors bg-transparent" />
            
            {/* CENTER */}
            <Panel minSize={30} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-900"> 
                 {/* Added bg-white to ensure no transparency issues */}
                <MonacoWrapper language="python" code={code} onChange={(val) => setCode(val || '')} />
            </Panel>

            <PanelResizeHandle className="w-1 hover:bg-blue-500 transition-colors bg-transparent" />
            
            {/* RIGHT */}
            <Panel ref={rightPanelRef} defaultSize={30} minSize={20} collapsible onCollapse={() => setRightCollapsed(true)} onExpand={() => setRightCollapsed(false)} className="border-l border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-800 bg-white dark:bg-gray-900">
                <AgentPanel />
            </Panel>
        </PanelGroup>
       </div>
     </div>
  );
}

src/features/editor/components/FileTree.tsx 
'use client';
import { useState } from 'react';
import { ChevronRight, ChevronDown, FileCode, Folder, FolderOpen } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

export interface FileNode {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'file' | 'folder';
  children?: FileNode[];
}

interface FileTreeProps {
  data: FileNode[];
  activeFileId: string | null;
  onSelect: (node: FileNode) => void;
  depth?: number;
}

export function FileTree({ data, activeFileId, onSelect, depth = 0 }: FileTreeProps) {
  return (
    <div className="w-full">
      {data.map((node) => (
        <FileTreeNode key={node.id} node={node} activeFileId={activeFileId} onSelect={onSelect} depth={depth} />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function FileTreeNode({ node, activeFileId, onSelect, depth }: any) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const isFolder = node.type === 'folder';
  const isActive = node.id === activeFileId;

  return (
    <div>
      <div
        className={cn(
          "flex items-center gap-1 py-1 px-2 cursor-pointer select-none transition-colors rounded-sm text-sm",
          isActive ? "bg-blue-100 text-blue-800" : "text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100",
        )}
        style={{ paddingLeft: `${depth * 12 + 4}px` }}
        onClick={(e) => {
          e.stopPropagation();
          onSelect(node); // Always select on click
          if (isFolder) setIsOpen(!isOpen); // Also toggle if it's a folder
        }}
      >
        <span className="shrink-0 text-gray-400">
          {isFolder ? (
            isOpen ? <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4" /> : <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
          ) : <span className="w-4 block" />}
        </span>

        <span className={cn("shrink-0", isFolder ? "text-blue-500" : "text-gray-500")}>
          {isFolder ? (isOpen ? <FolderOpen className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Folder className="w-4 h-4" />) : <FileCode className="w-4 h-4" />}
        </span>

        <span className="truncate">{node.name}</span>
      </div>

      {isFolder && isOpen && node.children && (
        <FileTree data={node.children} activeFileId={activeFileId} onSelect={onSelect} depth={depth + 1} />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

src/features/editor/components/MonacoWrapper.tsx
'use client';
import Editor, { useMonaco } from '@monaco-editor/react';
import { useTheme } from '@/context/ThemeContext';
import { useEffect } from 'react';

interface MonacoWrapperProps {
  code: string;
  language: string;
  onChange: (value: string | undefined) => void;
}

export function MonacoWrapper({ code, language, onChange }: MonacoWrapperProps) {
  const { theme } = useTheme();
  const monaco = useMonaco();

  // Determine the editor theme based on our app's theme
  const editorTheme = theme === 'dark' ? 'vs-dark' : 'light';

  useEffect(() => {
    if (monaco) {
      // Optional: Customizing the font to make it look modern
      monaco.editor.defineTheme('custom-dark', {
        base: 'vs-dark',
        inherit: true,
        rules: [],
        colors: {
          'editor.background': '#111827', // Matches Tailwind gray-900
        }
      });
    }
  }, [monaco]);

  return (
    <div className="h-full w-full overflow-hidden">
      <Editor
        height="100%"
        language={language.toLowerCase()}
        theme={editorTheme} // 👈 Dynamically switches theme
        value={code}
        onChange={onChange}
        options={{
          minimap: { enabled: false },
          fontSize: 14,
          fontFamily: "'Fira Code', 'Consolas', monospace",
          scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
          automaticLayout: true,
          padding: { top: 16 },
        }}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

import { apiClient } from '@/lib/api-client';
import type { ProjectFile } from '../types';

export const fileService = {
  getFiles: async (projectId: string): Promise<ProjectFile[]> => {
    const { data } = await apiClient.get(`/projects/${projectId}/files`);
    return data;
  },
  
  saveFile: async (fileId: string, content: string): Promise<void> => {
    await apiClient.put(`/files/${fileId}`, { content });
  }
};

src/lib/api-client.ts
// The Base URL of your Python Backend
const API_BASE_URL = 'http://localhost:8000';

export const apiClient = {
  // 1. Health Check
  getHealth: async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/`);
      return await res.json();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Backend offline:", error);
      return { status: "offline" };
    }
  },

  // 2. Transcribe Audio (Mic -> Backend -> Gladia)
  transcribeAudio: async (audioBlob: Blob) => {
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('file', audioBlob, 'recording.wav');

    // Note: This matches the "Voice Router" we built: /api/voice/process
    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/voice/process`, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData, 
    });
    
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Transcription failed");
    return await res.json();
  },

  // 3. Execute Agent (Text -> Backend -> OpenAI -> Code)
  executeAgent: async (instruction: string, filename: string, fileContent: string) => {
    const res = await fetch(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/agent/execute`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        instruction,
        filename,
        file_content: fileContent
      }),
    });

    if (!res.ok) {
      throw new Error('AI execution failed');
    }
    
    return await res.json();
  }
};

src/lib/utils.ts
import { type ClassValue, clsx } from 'clsx';
import { twMerge } from 'tailwind-merge';

/**
 * Merges Tailwind classes safely.
 * Example: cn("px-2 py-1 bg-red-500", "bg-blue-500") -> "px-2 py-1 bg-blue-500"
 * This prevents the "CSS Cascade" headache where styles don't apply.
 */
export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}

/**
 * Simulates a delay (useful for testing loading states without a backend).
 */
export function delay(ms: number) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

   /// <reference types="next" />
/// <reference types="next/image-types/global" />

// NOTE: This file should not be edited
